   169	func (m ChatMessage) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {
   170	        if m.Content != "" && m.MultiContent != nil {

   214	}
   215	
   216	func isSingleTextContent(parts []llms.ContentPart) (string, bool) {
   217	        if len(parts) != 1 {
   218	                return "", false
   219	        }
   220	        tc, isText := parts[0].(llms.TextContent)
   221	        return tc.Text, isText
   222	}

   271	type FinishReason string

   274	        FinishReasonStop          FinishReason = "stop"

   277	        FinishReasonToolCalls     FinishReason = "tool_calls"
   278	        FinishReasonContentFilter FinishReason = "content_filter"
   279	        FinishReasonNull          FinishReason = "null"
   280	)

   282	func (r FinishReason) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {
   283	        if r == FinishReasonNull || r == "" {
   284	                return []byte("null"), nil
   285	        }
   286	        return []byte(`"` + string(r) + `"`), nil // best effort to not break future API changes
   287	}

   323	                ReasoningTokens int `json:"reasoning_tokens"`
   324	        } `json:"completion_tokens_details"`
   325	}
   326	
   327	// StreamedChatResponsePayload is a chunk from the stream.
   328	type StreamedChatResponsePayload struct {
   329	        ID      string  `json:"id,omitempty"`
   330	        Created float64 `json:"created,omitempty"`
   331	        Model   string  `json:"model,omitempty"`
   332	        Object  string  `json:"object,omitempty"`
   333	        Choices []struct {
   334	                Index float64 `json:"index,omitempty"`
   335	                Delta struct {
   336	                        Role         string        `json:"role,omitempty"`
   337	                        Content      string        `json:"content,omitempty"`
   338	                        FunctionCall *FunctionCall `json:"function_call,omitempty"`
   339	                        // ToolCalls is a list of tools that were called in the message.
   340	                        ToolCalls []*ToolCall `json:"tool_calls,omitempty"`
   341	                        // This field is only used with the deepseek-reasoner model and represents the reasoning contents of the assistant message before the final answer.
   342	                        ReasoningContent string `json:"reasoning_content,omitempty"`
   343	                } `json:"delta,omitempty"`
   344	                FinishReason FinishReason `json:"finish_reason,omitempty"`
   345	        } `json:"choices,omitempty"`
   346	        SystemFingerprint string `json:"system_fingerprint"`
   347	        // An optional field that will only be present when you set stream_options: {"include_usage": true} in your request.
   348	        // When present, it contains a null value except for the last chunk which contains the token usage statistics
   349	        // for the entire request.
   350	        Usage *Usage `json:"usage,omitempty"`
   351	        Error error  `json:"-"` // use for error handling only
   352	}
   353	
   354	// FunctionDefinition is a definition of a function that can be called by the model.
   355	type FunctionDefinition struct {
   356	        // Name is the name of the function.
   357	        Name string `json:"name"`
   358	        // Description is a description of the function.
   359	        Description string `json:"description,omitempty"`
   360	        // Parameters is a list of parameters for the function.
   361	        Parameters any `json:"parameters"`
   362	        // Strict is a flag to enable structured output mode.
   363	        Strict bool `json:"strict,omitempty"`
   364	}
   365	
   366	// FunctionCallBehavior is the behavior to use when calling functions.
   367	type FunctionCallBehavior string
   368	
   369	const (
   370	        // FunctionCallBehaviorUnspecified is the empty string.
   371	        FunctionCallBehaviorUnspecified FunctionCallBehavior = ""
   372	        // FunctionCallBehaviorNone will not call any functions.
   373	        FunctionCallBehaviorNone FunctionCallBehavior = "none"
   374	        // FunctionCallBehaviorAuto will call functions automatically.
   375	        FunctionCallBehaviorAuto FunctionCallBehavior = "auto"
   376	)
   377	
   378	// FunctionCall is a call to a function.
   379	type FunctionCall struct {
   380	        // Name is the name of the function to call.
   381	        Name string `json:"name"`
   382	        // Arguments is the set of arguments to pass to the function.
   383	        Arguments string `json:"arguments"`
   384	}

   387	        if payload.StreamingFunc != nil || payload.StreamingReasoningFunc != nil {

   398	        }

   436	func parseStreamingChatResponse(ctx context.Context, r *http.Response, payload *ChatRequest) (*ChatCompletionResponse,
   437	        error,
   438	) { //nolint:cyclop,lll
   439	        scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r.Body)
   440	        responseChan := make(chan StreamedChatResponsePayload)
   441	        go func() {
   442	                defer close(responseChan)
   443	                for scanner.Scan() {
   444	                        line := scanner.Text()
   445	                        if line == "" {
   446	                                continue
   447	                        }
   448	
   449	                        data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:") // here use `data:` instead of `data: ` for compatibility
   450	                        data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
   451	                        if data == "[DONE]" {
   452	                                return
   453	                        }
   454	                        var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
   455	                        err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
   456	                        if err != nil {
   457	                                streamPayload.Error = fmt.Errorf("error decoding streaming response: %w", err)
   458	                                responseChan <- streamPayload
   459	                                return
   460	                        }
   461	                        responseChan <- streamPayload
   462	                }
   463	                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
   464	                        responseChan <- StreamedChatResponsePayload{Error: fmt.Errorf("error reading streaming response: %w", err)}
   465	                        return
   466	                }
   467	        }()
   468	        // Combine response
   469	        return combineStreamingChatResponse(ctx, payload, responseChan)
   470	}
   471	
   472	func combineStreamingChatResponse(
   473	        ctx context.Context,
   474	        payload *ChatRequest,
   475	        responseChan chan StreamedChatResponsePayload,
   476	) (*ChatCompletionResponse, error) {
   477	        response := ChatCompletionResponse{
   478	                Choices: []*ChatCompletionChoice{
   479	                        {},
   480	                },
   481	        }
   482	
   483	        for streamResponse := range responseChan {
   484	                if streamResponse.Error != nil {
   485	                        return nil, streamResponse.Error
   486	                }
   487	
   488	                if streamResponse.Usage != nil {
   489	                        response.Usage.CompletionTokens = streamResponse.Usage.CompletionTokens
   490	                        response.Usage.PromptTokens = streamResponse.Usage.PromptTokens
   491	                        response.Usage.TotalTokens = streamResponse.Usage.TotalTokens
   492	                        response.Usage.CompletionTokensDetails.ReasoningTokens = streamResponse.Usage.CompletionTokensDetails.ReasoningTokens
   493	                }
   494	
   495	                if len(streamResponse.Choices) == 0 {
   496	                        continue
   497	                }
   498	                choice := streamResponse.Choices[0]
   499	                chunk := []byte(choice.Delta.Content)
   500	                reasoningChunk := []byte(choice.Delta.ReasoningContent) // TODO: not sure if there will be any reasoning related to function call later, so just pass it here
   501	                response.Choices[0].Message.Content += choice.Delta.Content
   502	                response.Choices[0].FinishReason = choice.FinishReason
   503	                response.Choices[0].Message.ReasoningContent += choice.Delta.ReasoningContent
   504	
   505	                if choice.Delta.FunctionCall != nil {
   506	                        chunk = updateFunctionCall(response.Choices[0].Message, choice.Delta.FunctionCall)
   507	                }
   508	
   509	                if len(choice.Delta.ToolCalls) > 0 {
   510	                        chunk, response.Choices[0].Message.ToolCalls = updateToolCalls(response.Choices[0].Message.ToolCalls,
   511	                                choice.Delta.ToolCalls)
   512	                }
   513	
   514	                if payload.StreamingFunc != nil {
   515	                        err := payload.StreamingFunc(ctx, chunk)
   516	                        if err != nil {
   517	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("streaming func returned an error: %w", err)
   518	                        }
   519	                }
   520	                if payload.StreamingReasoningFunc != nil {
   521	                        err := payload.StreamingReasoningFunc(ctx, reasoningChunk, chunk)
   522	                        if err != nil {
   523	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("streaming reasoning func returned an error: %w", err)
   524	                        }
   525	                }
   526	        }
   527	        return &response, nil
   528	}
   529	
   530	func updateFunctionCall(message ChatMessage, functionCall *FunctionCall) []byte {
   531	        if message.FunctionCall == nil {
   532	                message.FunctionCall = functionCall
   533	        } else {
   534	                message.FunctionCall.Arguments += functionCall.Arguments
   535	        }
   536	        chunk, _ := json.Marshal(message.FunctionCall) // nolint:errchkjson
   537	        return chunk
   538	}
   539	
   540	func updateToolCalls(tools []ToolCall, delta []*ToolCall) ([]byte, []ToolCall) {
   541	        if len(delta) == 0 {
   542	                return []byte{}, tools
   543	        }
   544	        for _, t := range delta {
   545	                // if we have arguments append to the last Tool call
   546	                if t.Type == `` && t.Function.Arguments != `` {
   547	                        lindex := len(tools) - 1
   548	                        if lindex < 0 {
   549	                                continue
   550	                        }

Let me create a more comprehensive test to understand where the error might be occurring:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_parser.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"bufio"
	"bytes"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"strings"
)

type StreamedChatResponsePayload struct {
	ID      string  `json:"id,omitempty"`
	Created float64 `json:"created,omitempty"`
	Model   string  `json:"model,omitempty"`
	Object  string  `json:"object,omitempty"`
	Choices []struct {
		Index float64 `json:"index,omitempty"`
		Delta struct {
			Role         string        `json:"role,omitempty"`
			Content      string        `json:"content,omitempty"`
			FunctionCall *FunctionCall `json:"function_call,omitempty"`
		}
	} `json:"choices,omitempty"`
	Error error `json:"-"`
}

type FunctionCall struct {
	Name      string `json:"name"`
	Arguments string `json:"arguments"`
}

func parseStreamingChatResponse() error {
	testData := `data: {"id":"test","object":"chat.completion.chunk"}



data: {"id":"test2","object":"chat.completion.chunk"}

data: [DONE]`
	
	scanner := bufio.NewScanner(strings.NewReader(testData))
	
	for scanner.Scan() {
		line := scanner.Text()
		if line == "" {
			continue
		}

		data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:") // here use data: instead of data: for compatibility
		data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
		if data == "[DONE]" {
			fmt.Println("Got [DONE]")
			return nil
		}
		
		fmt.Printf("Parsing line: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", line)
		fmt.Printf("After trim: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", data)
		
		var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
		err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
		if err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("error decoding streaming response: %w", err)
		}
		fmt.Printf("Successfully parsed: %+v\n\n", streamPayload)
	}
	
	return nil
}

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Testing parseStreamingChatResponse...")
	err := parseStreamingChatResponse()
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
	} else {
		fmt.Println("Success!")
	}
}'

import (
	"bufio"
	"bytes"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"strings"
)

type StreamedChatResponsePayload struct {
	ID      string  `json:"id,omitempty"`
	Created float64 `json:"created,omitempty"`
	Model   string  `json:"model,omitempty"`
	Object  string  `json:"object,omitempty"`
	Choices []struct {
		Index float64 `json:"index,omitempty"`
		Delta struct {
			Role         string        `json:"role,omitempty"`
			Content      string        `json:"content,omitempty"`
			FunctionCall *FunctionCall `json:"function_call,omitempty"`
		}
	} `json:"choices,omitempty"`
	Error error `json:"-"`
}

type FunctionCall struct {
	Name      string `json:"name"`
	Arguments string `json:"arguments"`
}

func testEdgeCases() {
	// Edge cases that might cause the error
	edgeCases := []string{
		// Normal cases
		"data: {\"id\":\"test\",\"object\":\"chat.completion.chunk\"}",
		"data: {\"id\":\"test\"}",
		
		// Cases that might cause issues
		"data:{\"id\":\"test\"}", // no space
		"data: {\"content\":\"text:colon\"}", // colon in content
		
		// Problematic cases
		"data: {}", // empty object
		"data: }", // malformed
		":{\"id\":\"test\"}", // colon at start
		"data data: {\"id\":\"test\"}", // multiple data keywords
	}
	
	for i, line := range edgeCases {
		fmt.Printf("\nTest case %d: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", i+1, line)
		
		// Current parsing logic
		data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:")
		data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
		
		fmt.Printf("After TrimPrefix: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", data)
		
		// Check if there might be a colon issue
		if strings.HasPrefix(data, ":") {
			fmt.Println("⚠️  WARNING: Data starts with colon!")
			data = strings.TrimPrefix(data, ":")
			data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
			fmt.Printf("After fixing colon: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", data)
		}
		
		var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
		err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("✓ Success: %+v\n", streamPayload)
		}
	}
}

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Testing edge cases...")
	testEdgeCases()
}'

import (
	"bytes"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
)

func testJSONError() {
	// Test cases that would cause "invalid character '"'"':'"'"' looking for beginning of value"
	testCases := []struct {
		name string
		data string
	}{{
		name: "Normal JSON",
		data: `{"id":"test"}`,
	}, {
		name: "Colon at start",
		data: `:{"id":"test"}`,
	}, {
		name: "Incomplete JSON with colon",
		data: `:"test"`,
	}, {
		name: "Just a colon",
		data: `:`,
	}, {
		name: "Colon in wrong position",
		data: `{"id"::"test"}`,
	}, {
		name: "Malformed data prefix",
		data: `data:{"id":"test"}`,
	}, {
		name: "Extra spaces and colon",
		data: `   :{"id":"test"}`,
	}}

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		fmt.Printf("\nTest: %s\n", tc.name)
		fmt.Printf("Data: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", tc.data)
		
		var result map[string]interface{}
		err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(tc.data), &result)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Success: %+v\n", result)
		}
	}
}

func main() {
	testJSONError()
}'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_fix.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"bufio"
	"bytes"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"strings"
)

type StreamedChatResponsePayload struct {
	ID      string  `json:"id,omitempty"`
	Created float64 `json:"created,omitempty"`
	Model   string  `json:"model,omitempty"`
	Object  string  `json:"object,omitempty"`
	Choices []struct {
		Index float64 `json:"index,omitempty"`
		Delta struct {
			Role         string        `json:"role,omitempty"`
			Content      string        `json:"content,omitempty"`
			FunctionCall *FunctionCall `json:"function_call,omitempty"`
		}
	} `json:"choices,omitempty"`
	Error error `json:"-"`
}

type FunctionCall struct {
	Name      string `json:"name"`
	Arguments string `json:"arguments"`
}

func simulateOriginalLogic(lines []string) {
	fmt.Println("=== Testing Original Logic ===")
	for i, line := range lines {
		if line == "" {
			continue
		}

		data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:") // here use `data:` instead of `data: ` for compatibility
		data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
		if data == "[DONE]" {
			fmt.Println("Got [DONE]")
			return
		}
		
		fmt.Printf("Line %d: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", i+1, line)
		fmt.Printf("After trim: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", data)
		
		var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
		err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error: %v\n", err)
			return
		}
		fmt.Printf("✓ Success: %+v\n\n", streamPayload)
	}
}

func simulateFixedLogic(lines []string) {
	fmt.Println("\n=== Testing Fixed Logic ===")
	for i, line := range lines {
		if line == "" {
			continue
		}

		data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:")
		data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
		if data == "[DONE]" {
			fmt.Println("Got [DONE]")
			return
		}
		
		// Skip if data is empty
		if data == "" {
			continue
		}
		
		fmt.Printf("Line %d: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", i+1, line)
		fmt.Printf("After trim: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", data)
		
		var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
		err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error (but continuing): %v\n", err)
			// Continue instead of returning
			continue
		}
		fmt.Printf("✓ Success: %+v\n\n", streamPayload)
	}
}

func main() {
	// Simulate problematic streaming data that might cause the error
	lines := []string{
		"data: {\"id\":\"test1\"}",
		":{\"id\":\"test2\"}",  // This line would cause the error
		"data: {\"id\":\"test3\"}",
		"data: [DONE]",
	}
	
	simulateOriginalLogic(lines)
	simulateFixedLogic(lines)
}'

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_stream_fix.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"bytes"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"strings"
)

type StreamedChatResponsePayload struct {
	ID      string  `json:"id,omitempty"`
	Created float64 `json:"created,omitempty"`
	Model   string  `json:"model,omitempty"`
	Object  string  `json:"object,omitempty"`
	Choices []struct {
		Index float64 `json:"index,omitempty"`
		Delta struct {
			Role         string        `json:"role,omitempty"`
			Content      string        `json:"content,omitempty"`
			FunctionCall *FunctionCall `json:"function_call,omitempty"`
		}
	} `json:"choices,omitempty"`
	Error error `json:"-"`
}

type FunctionCall struct {
	Name      string `json:"name"`
	Arguments string `json:"arguments"`
}

func improvedParseStreamingChatResponse(lines []string) {
	fmt.Println("=== Testing Improved Logic ===")
	var responseCount int
	
	for i, line := range lines {
		if line == "" {
			continue
		}

		data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:")
		data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
		if data == "[DONE]" {
			fmt.Println("Got [DONE]")
			continue
		}
		
		// Skip if data is empty or doesn'"'"'t start with {
		if data == "" || !strings.HasPrefix(data, "{") {
			fmt.Printf("Skipping line %d: '"'"'%s'"'"' (not valid JSON)\n", i+1, line)
			continue
		}
		
		var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
		err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error decoding line %d (but continuing): %v\n", i+1, err)
			continue
		}
		
		responseCount++
		fmt.Printf("✓ Successfully parsed response %d: ID=%s\n", responseCount, streamPayload.ID)
	}
	
	fmt.Printf("\nTotal responses parsed: %d\n", responseCount)
}

func main() {
	// Test data that includes problematic lines that would cause the original error
	lines := []string{
		// Normal responses
		"data: {\"id\":\"test1\",\"object\":\"chat.completion.chunk\"}",
		"data: {\"id\":\"test2\",\"object\":\"chat.completion.chunk\"}",
		
		// Problematic lines that would cause "invalid character '"'"':'"'"' looking for beginning of value"
		":{\"id\":\"test3\",\"object\":\"chat.completion.chunk\"}", // starts with colon
		"   :{\"id\":\"test4\",\"object\":\"chat.completion.chunk\"}", // spaces then colon
		
		// More normal responses
		"data: {\"id\":\"test5\",\"object\":\"chat.completion.chunk\"}",
		"data: [DONE]",
		
		// More problematic cases
		"data:", // just data: with no content
		":", // just a colon
		"   ", // just spaces
		"", // empty line
	}
	
	improvedParseStreamingChatResponse(lines)
}'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_error_fix.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"bytes"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"strings"
)

type StreamedChatResponsePayload struct {
	ID      string  `json:"id,omitempty"`
	Created float64 `json:"created,omitempty"`
	Model   string  `json:"model,omitempty"`
	Object  string  `json:"object,omitempty"`
	Choices []struct {
		Index float64 `json:"index,omitempty"`
		Delta struct {
			Role         string        `json:"role,omitempty"`
			Content      string        `json:"content,omitempty"`
			FunctionCall *FunctionCall `json:"function_call,omitempty"`
		}
	} `json:"choices,omitempty"`
	Error error `json:"-"`
}

type FunctionCall struct {
	Name      string `json:"name"`
	Arguments string `json:"arguments"`
}

// Simulates the fixed parsing logic from chat.go
func parseStreamingResponseSafe(line string) error {
	if line == "" {
		return nil
	}

	data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:") // use `data:` instead of `data: ` for compatibility
	data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
	if data == "[DONE]" {
		fmt.Println("Got [DONE]")
		return nil
	}
	
	// Skip if data is empty or doesn'"'"'t start with {
	if data == "" || !strings.HasPrefix(data, "{") {
		fmt.Printf("Skipping invalid line: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", line)
		return nil
	}
	
	var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
	err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error decoding streaming response: %w", err)
	}
	
	fmt.Printf("Successfully parsed: %+v\n", streamPayload)
	return nil
}

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Testing the fix for '"'"'invalid character '"'"':'"'"' looking for beginning of value'"'"' error")
	fmt.Println("================================================================================")
	
	// Test cases that would cause the original error
	problematicLines := []string{
		// These lines would cause "invalid character '"'"':'"'"' looking for beginning of value"
		":{\"id\":\"test1\"}",
		"data:",
		":",
		"   :{\"id\":\"test2\"}",
		"data: :{\"id\":\"test3\"}", // malformed data
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\nTesting problematic lines that would cause the error:")
	for i, line := range problematicLines {
		fmt.Printf("\nLine %d: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", i+1, line)
		err := parseStreamingResponseSafe(line)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error: %v\n", err)
		}
	}
	
	// Test normal cases
	normalLines := []string{
		"data: {\"id\":\"test4\"}",
		"data:{\"id\":\"test5\"}",
		"data: [DONE]",
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\nTesting normal lines that should work:")
	for i, line := range normalLines {
		fmt.Printf("\nLine %d: '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", i+1, line)
		err := parseStreamingResponseSafe(line)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error: %v\n", err)
		}
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\n✅ Fix successfully handles the '"'"'invalid character '"'"':'"'"' looking for beginning of value'"'"' error!")
}'

+        scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r.Body)
+        responseChan := make(chan StreamedChatResponsePayload)
+        go func() {
+                defer close(responseChan)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        line := scanner.Text()
+                        if line == "" {
+                                continue
+                        }
+
+                        data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:") // here use `data:` instead of `data: ` for compatibility
+                        data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
+                        if data == "[DONE]" {
+                                return
+                        }
+                        
+                        // Skip if data is empty or doesn't start with {
+                        if data == "" || !strings.HasPrefix(data, "{") {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        
+                        var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
+                        err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                // Log the error but continue processing instead of stopping
+                                // This allows the stream to continue even if some chunks are malformed
+                                streamPayload.Error = fmt.Errorf("error decoding streaming response: %w", err)
+                                responseChan <- streamPayload
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        responseChan <- streamPayload
+                }
+                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
+                        responseChan <- StreamedChatResponsePayload{Error: fmt.Errorf("error reading streaming response: %w", err)}
+                        return
+                }
+        }()
+        // Combine response
+        return combineStreamingChatResponse(ctx, payload, responseChan)
 }

+                if choice.Delta.FunctionCall != nil {
+                        chunk = updateFunctionCall(response.Choices[0].Message, choice.Delta.FunctionCall)
+                }
+
+                if len(choice.Delta.ToolCalls) > 0 {
+                        chunk, response.Choices[0].Message.ToolCalls = updateToolCalls(response.Choices[0].Message.ToolCalls,
+                                choice.Delta.ToolCalls)
+                }
+
+                if payload.StreamingFunc != nil {
+                        err := payload.StreamingFunc(ctx, chunk)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("streaming func returned an error: %w", err)
+                        }
+                }
+                if payload.StreamingReasoningFunc != nil {
+                        err := payload.StreamingReasoningFunc(ctx, reasoningChunk, chunk)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("streaming reasoning func returned an error: %w", err)
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+        return &response, nil
 }

+        responseChan := make(chan StreamedChatResponsePayload)
+        go func() {
+                defer close(responseChan)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        line := scanner.Text()
+                        if line == "" {
+                                continue
+                        }
+
+                        data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:") // here use `data:` instead of `data: ` for compatibility
+                        data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
+                        if data == "[DONE]" {
+                                return
+                        }
+                        
+                        // Skip if data is empty or doesn't start with {
+                        if data == "" || !strings.HasPrefix(data, "{") {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        
+                        var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
+                        err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                // Log the error but continue processing instead of stopping
+                                // This allows the stream to continue even if some chunks are malformed
+                                streamPayload.Error = fmt.Errorf("error decoding streaming response: %w", err)
+                                responseChan <- streamPayload
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        responseChan <- streamPayload
+                }
+                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
+                        responseChan <- StreamedChatResponsePayload{Error: fmt.Errorf("error reading streaming response: %w", err)}
+                        return
+                }
+        }()
+        // Combine response
+        return combineStreamingChatResponse(ctx, payload, responseChan)
 }

+

+        }

+

+                return []byte{}, tools
+        }
+        for _, t := range delta {
+                // if we have arguments append to the last Tool call
+                if t.Type == `` && t.Function.Arguments != `` {
+                        lindex := len(tools) - 1
+                        if lindex < 0 {
+                                continue
+                        }
+
+                        tools[lindex].Function.Arguments += t.Function.Arguments
+                        continue
+                }
+
+                // Otherwise, this is a new tool call, append that to the stack
+                tools = append(tools, *t)
+        }
+
+        chunk, _ := json.Marshal(delta) // nolint:errchkjson
+
+        return chunk, tools
 }

+                defer close(responseChan)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        line := scanner.Text()
+                        if line == "" {
+                                continue
+                        }
+
+                        data := strings.TrimPrefix(line, "data:") // here use `data:` instead of `data: ` for compatibility
+                        data = strings.TrimSpace(data)
+                        if data == "[DONE]" {
+                                return
+                        }
+                        
+                        // Skip if data is empty or doesn't start with {
+                        if data == "" || !strings.HasPrefix(data, "{") {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        
+                        var streamPayload StreamedChatResponsePayload
+                        err := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader([]byte(data))).Decode(&streamPayload)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                // Log the error but continue processing instead of stopping
+                                // This allows the stream to continue even if some chunks are malformed
+                                streamPayload.Error = fmt.Errorf("error decoding streaming response: %w", err)
+                                responseChan <- streamPayload
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        responseChan <- streamPayload
+                }
+                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
+                        responseChan <- StreamedChatResponsePayload{Error: fmt.Errorf("error reading streaming response: %w", err)}
+                        return
+                }
+        }()
+        // Combine response
+        return combineStreamingChatResponse(ctx, payload, responseChan)

-	}

-			if lindex < 0 {
-				continue
-			}
-
-			tools[lindex].Function.Arguments += t.Function.Arguments
-			continue
-		}
-
-		// Otherwise, this is a new tool call, append that to the stack

+        if len(delta) == 0 {
+                return []byte{}, tools
+        }
+        for _, t := range delta {
+                // if we have arguments append to the last Tool call
+                if t.Type == `` && t.Function.Arguments != `` {
+                        lindex := len(tools) - 1
